    <script>
     $(document).ready(function () {
 	var userLang = navigator.language || navigator.userLanguage;
     var pre = userLang.split('-')[0];
     if (pre != "de") {
     	
     	var country = "";
 
         if (Cookies.get('checkedLocation') != "checked") {
 
             $.getJSON('https://timezoneapi.io/api/ip', function (data) {
 
                 // Request OK?
                 if (data.meta.code == '200') {
                     country = data.data.country;
                     country_code = data.data.country_code;
                     var europe = ['BG', 'HR', 'LU', 'EE', 'FI', 'GR', 'HU', 'IE', 'IT', 'LV', 'LT', 'MT', 'CZ', 'RO', 'SK', 'SI', 'ES', 'SE', 'GB'];
 
                     if ($.inArray(country_code, europe) > -1) {
                         Cookies.set('isInEurope', 'yes');
                         $("#lang_location").show();
                         setDialog();
                     }
 
                     Cookies.set('checkedLocation', 'checked');
                 }
             });
         }
     } else {
     	if (Cookies.get('isInEurope') == 'yes') {
                 $("#lang_location").show();
                 setDialog();
             }
     }
     
     function setDialog() {
        if (Cookies.get('dialogSeen') != 'done') {
 					$('#geoModal').modal('show');
 					Cookies.set('dialogSeen', 'done');
                 }
         	}
 });
    </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
 	
 function sortAscending(a, b) {
     var date1 = $(a).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date1 = new Date(date1[2], date1[1] - 1, date1[0]);
     var date2 = $(b).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date2 = new Date(date2[2], date2[1] - 1, date2[0]);
     return (date1 > date2) ? -1 : (date1 < date2) ? 1 : 0;
 }
 
 $('#termine .termin').sort(sortAscending).appendTo('#termine'); 
 
 var myDate=new Date();
 myDate.setDate(myDate.getDate() - 5); 
    
 $( ".termin" ).each(function() {
 var date3 = $(this).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
 date3 = new Date(date3[2], date3[1] - 1, date3[0]);
   
 if (date3 > myDate ) {
 this.style.display = "flex";
 }
 
 }); 
 
 // Promoslider

    <script>
     $(document).ready(function () {
 	var userLang = navigator.language || navigator.userLanguage;
     var pre = userLang.split('-')[0];
     if (pre != "de") {
     	
     	var country = "";
 
         if (Cookies.get('checkedLocation') != "checked") {
 
             $.getJSON('https://timezoneapi.io/api/ip', function (data) {
 
                 // Request OK?
                 if (data.meta.code == '200') {
                     country = data.data.country;
                     country_code = data.data.country_code;
                     var europe = ['BG', 'HR', 'LU', 'EE', 'FI', 'GR', 'HU', 'IE', 'IT', 'LV', 'LT', 'MT', 'CZ', 'RO', 'SK', 'SI', 'ES', 'SE', 'GB'];
 
                     if ($.inArray(country_code, europe) > -1) {
                         Cookies.set('isInEurope', 'yes');
                         $("#lang_location").show();
                         setDialog();
                     }
 
                     Cookies.set('checkedLocation', 'checked');
                 }
             });
         }
     } else {
     	if (Cookies.get('isInEurope') == 'yes') {
                 $("#lang_location").show();
                 setDialog();
             }
     }
     
     function setDialog() {
        if (Cookies.get('dialogSeen') != 'done') {
 					$('#geoModal').modal('show');
 					Cookies.set('dialogSeen', 'done');
                 }
         	}
 });
    </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
 	
 function sortAscending(a, b) {
     var date1 = $(a).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date1 = new Date(date1[2], date1[1] - 1, date1[0]);
     var date2 = $(b).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date2 = new Date(date2[2], date2[1] - 1, date2[0]);
     return (date1 > date2) ? -1 : (date1 < date2) ? 1 : 0;
 }
 
 $('#termine .termin').sort(sortAscending).appendTo('#termine'); 
 
 var myDate=new Date();
 myDate.setDate(myDate.getDate() - 5); 
    
 $( ".termin" ).each(function() {
 var date3 = $(this).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
 date3 = new Date(date3[2], date3[1] - 1, date3[0]);
   
 if (date3 > myDate ) {
 this.style.display = "flex";
 }
 
 });

    <script>
     $(document).ready(function () {
 	var userLang = navigator.language || navigator.userLanguage;
     var pre = userLang.split('-')[0];
     if (pre != "de") {
     	
     	var country = "";
 
         if (Cookies.get('checkedLocation') != "checked") {
 
             $.getJSON('https://timezoneapi.io/api/ip', function (data) {
 
                 // Request OK?
                 if (data.meta.code == '200') {
                     country = data.data.country;
                     country_code = data.data.country_code;
                     var europe = ['BG', 'HR', 'LU', 'EE', 'FI', 'GR', 'HU', 'IE', 'IT', 'LV', 'LT', 'MT', 'CZ', 'RO', 'SK', 'SI', 'ES', 'SE', 'GB'];
 
                     if ($.inArray(country_code, europe) > -1) {
                         Cookies.set('isInEurope', 'yes');
                         $("#lang_location").show();
                         setDialog();
                     }
 
                     Cookies.set('checkedLocation', 'checked');
                 }
             });
         }
     } else {
     	if (Cookies.get('isInEurope') == 'yes') {
                 $("#lang_location").show();
                 setDialog();
             }
     }
     
     function setDialog() {
        if (Cookies.get('dialogSeen') != 'done') {
 					$('#geoModal').modal('show');
 					Cookies.set('dialogSeen', 'done');
                 }
         	}
 });
    </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
 	
 function sortAscending(a, b) {
     var date1 = $(a).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date1 = new Date(date1[2], date1[1] - 1, date1[0]);
     var date2 = $(b).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date2 = new Date(date2[2], date2[1] - 1, date2[0]);
     return (date1 > date2) ? -1 : (date1 < date2) ? 1 : 0;
 }
 
 $('#termine .termin').sort(sortAscending).appendTo('#termine'); 
 
 var myDate=new Date();
 myDate.setDate(myDate.getDate() - 5); 
    
 $( ".termin" ).each(function() {
 var date3 = $(this).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
 date3 = new Date(date3[2], date3[1] - 1, date3[0]);
   
 if (date3 > myDate ) {
 this.style.display = "flex";
 }
 
 }); 
 
 // Promoslider

         //fx:'fade',

 }).css("display","block");

       <h3 class="eKomi_header">
        Kundenbewertung
       </h3>
       <div class="margin-top-1 margin-bottom-2" id="eKomiWidget_default">

       <div class="margin-top-1 margin-bottom-2 aside hidden-xs hidden-sm">

    <script>
     $(document).ready(function () {
 	var userLang = navigator.language || navigator.userLanguage;
     var pre = userLang.split('-')[0];
     if (pre != "de") {
     	
     	var country = "";
 
         if (Cookies.get('checkedLocation') != "checked") {
 
             $.getJSON('https://timezoneapi.io/api/ip', function (data) {
 
                 // Request OK?
                 if (data.meta.code == '200') {
                     country = data.data.country;
                     country_code = data.data.country_code;
                     var europe = ['BG', 'HR', 'LU', 'EE', 'FI', 'GR', 'HU', 'IE', 'IT', 'LV', 'LT', 'MT', 'CZ', 'RO', 'SK', 'SI', 'ES', 'SE', 'GB'];
 
                     if ($.inArray(country_code, europe) > -1) {
                         Cookies.set('isInEurope', 'yes');
                         $("#lang_location").show();
                         setDialog();
                     }
 
                     Cookies.set('checkedLocation', 'checked');
                 }
             });
         }
     } else {
     	if (Cookies.get('isInEurope') == 'yes') {
                 $("#lang_location").show();
                 setDialog();
             }
     }
     
     function setDialog() {
        if (Cookies.get('dialogSeen') != 'done') {
 					$('#geoModal').modal('show');
 					Cookies.set('dialogSeen', 'done');
                 }
         	}
 });
    </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
 	
 function sortAscending(a, b) {
     var date1 = $(a).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date1 = new Date(date1[2], date1[1] - 1, date1[0]);
     var date2 = $(b).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date2 = new Date(date2[2], date2[1] - 1, date2[0]);
     return (date1 > date2) ? -1 : (date1 < date2) ? 1 : 0;
 }
 
 $('#termine .termin').sort(sortAscending).appendTo('#termine'); 
 
 var myDate=new Date();
 myDate.setDate(myDate.getDate() - 5); 
    
 $( ".termin" ).each(function() {
 var date3 = $(this).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
 date3 = new Date(date3[2], date3[1] - 1, date3[0]);
   
 if (date3 > myDate ) {
 this.style.display = "flex";
 }
 
 });

     $(document).ready(function () {
 	var userLang = navigator.language || navigator.userLanguage;
     var pre = userLang.split('-')[0];
     if (pre != "de") {
     	
     	var country = "";
 
         if (Cookies.get('checkedLocation') != "checked") {
 
             $.getJSON('https://timezoneapi.io/api/ip', function (data) {
 
                 // Request OK?
                 if (data.meta.code == '200') {
                     country = data.data.country;
                     country_code = data.data.country_code;
                     var europe = ['BG', 'HR', 'LU', 'EE', 'FI', 'GR', 'HU', 'IE', 'IT', 'LV', 'LT', 'MT', 'CZ', 'RO', 'SK', 'SI', 'ES', 'SE', 'GB'];
 
                     if ($.inArray(country_code, europe) > -1) {
                         Cookies.set('isInEurope', 'yes');
                         $("#lang_location").show();
                         setDialog();
                     }
 
                     Cookies.set('checkedLocation', 'checked');
                 }
             });
         }
     } else {
     	if (Cookies.get('isInEurope') == 'yes') {
                 $("#lang_location").show();
                 setDialog();
             }
     }
     
     function setDialog() {
        if (Cookies.get('dialogSeen') != 'done') {
 					$('#geoModal').modal('show');
 					Cookies.set('dialogSeen', 'done');
                 }
         	}
 });
    </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
 	
 function sortAscending(a, b) {
     var date1 = $(a).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date1 = new Date(date1[2], date1[1] - 1, date1[0]);
     var date2 = $(b).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
     date2 = new Date(date2[2], date2[1] - 1, date2[0]);
     return (date1 > date2) ? -1 : (date1 < date2) ? 1 : 0;
 }
 
 $('#termine .termin').sort(sortAscending).appendTo('#termine'); 
 
 var myDate=new Date();
 myDate.setDate(myDate.getDate() - 5); 
    
 $( ".termin" ).each(function() {
 var date3 = $(this).find(".termin_date").text().split('.');
 date3 = new Date(date3[2], date3[1] - 1, date3[0]);
   
 if (date3 > myDate ) {
 this.style.display = "flex";
 }
 
 });
